● Everything is built, verified, and passing. Here's a summary:

  What was built

  A Dafny mechanisation of the paper's Package Calculus, with definitions,
  theorems, and tests separated as you asked:

  dfyconfig.toml   — project file: `dafny verify dfyconfig.toml` / `dafny test
  dfyconfig.toml`
  src/      (8 files) — definitions & executable functions
  lemmas/   (7 files) — machine-checked proofs of the paper's claims
  tests/    (1 file)  — 11 executable examples from the paper
  README.md           — paper-claim → lemma mapping, modelling choices, scope

  Verification status: 49 proof obligations, 0 errors, 0 assumes/axioms. All 11 
  tests pass.

  Paper claims verified with lemmas

  - Theorem 3.1.4 (NP-completeness) — both halves: membership (the validity
  predicate is compiled/executable, and AllResolutions carries a proven
  exactness contract), and hardness via the full Appendix B 3-SAT reduction
  (SatGivesResolution, ResolutionGivesSat, HardnessCorrect).
  - Definition 3.2.2's "partial order" claim — reflexivity, transitivity,
  antisymmetry. Notably, antisymmetry genuinely requires version uniqueness; on
  arbitrary package sets the ordering is only a preorder, which the lemma makes
  explicit.
  - Theorem 3.2.7 — correctness of the version-formula reduction.
  - Theorems 4.1.4 / 4.1.5 — soundness and completeness of the conflict
  reduction (the synthetic κ-package encoding), including the freshness
  conditions the paper leaves implicit.
  - §4.5, §4.8, §4.9 — package formulae subsume the core; optional dependencies
  affect only the build graph; singular dependencies embed into the core.
  - Theorems C.2 / C.3 — soundness and completeness of the SAT encoding.

  Tests

  Executable versions of the paper's examples: Figure 1 (unique resolution found
  by exhaustive search), Figure 3 (diamond problem — no resolution), the §3.2
  no-maximum example (two incomparable maximal resolutions), Figure 2 (conflicts
  + reduction round-trip), Example 4.8.3 (optional build edges), the SAT
  encoding of Figure 1, and live 3-SAT instances solved as resolution problems.

  Not mechanised (documented in README)

  The heavier reductions — concurrent versions (§4.2), peer deps (§4.3),
  features (§4.4), the Tseitin package-formula reduction, variable formulae
  (§4.6), virtual packages (§4.7), and the §5.2 composition theorems. These are
  natural follow-ups if you want to extend the development; the
  concurrent-versions reduction (§4.2) would be the most interesting next target
  since §5.2's composition results build on it.

✻ Sautéed for 23m 31s

❯ I definitely want implementations of the calculus with concurrent versions,   
  peer deps, and other features,                                                

● The big-ticket items. I'll add the remaining extensions one at a time, proving
  each reduction sound and complete before moving on: concurrent versions
  (§4.2), peer dependencies (§4.3), features (§4.4), then virtual packages
  (§4.7) and the Tseitin package-formula reduction (§4.5.4) as far as they'll
  go.

  First, the Name datatype needs constructors for the new synthetic names
  (granular names ⟨n,γ⟩, intermediates ⟨n,v,m⟩, feature packages ⟨n,f⟩, provider
  intermediates):

      102 +      else                                                    
      103 +        var orn := OrName(PNot(a), PNot(b));                  
      104 +        (set t | t in EncTargets(a, true) :: (Package(orn, 0),
          + t))                                                          
      105 +        + (set t | t in EncTargets(b, true) :: (Package(orn, 1
          +), t))                                                        
      106 +        + EncAuxEdges(a, true) + EncAuxEdges(b, true)         
      107 +    case POr(a, b) =>                                         
      108 +      if !neg then                                            
      109 +        var orn := OrName(a, b);                              
      110 +        (set t | t in EncTargets(a, false) :: (Package(orn, 0)
          +, t))                                                         
      111 +        + (set t | t in EncTargets(b, false) :: (Package(orn, 
          +1), t))                                                       
      112 +        + EncAuxEdges(a, false) + EncAuxEdges(b, false)       
      113 +      else EncAuxEdges(a, true) + EncAuxEdges(b, true)        
      114 +    case PNot(g) => EncAuxEdges(g, !neg)                      
      115 +  }                                                           
      116 +                                                              
      117 +  // The synthetic packages: two versions per disjunction subf
          +ormula                                                        
      118 +  // ((a)(iii)) and per negated atom ((a)(iv)).               
      119 +  function EncAuxRepo(f: PFormula, neg: bool): set<Package>   
      120 +    decreases FSize(f)                                        
      121 +  {                                                           
      122 +    match f                                                   
      123 +    case PAtom(n, vs) =>                                      
      124 +      if !neg then {}                                         
      125 +      else {Package(NegName(n, vs), 0), Package(NegName(n, vs)
          +, 1)}                                                         
      126 +    case PAnd(a, b) =>                                        
      127 +      if !neg then EncAuxRepo(a, false) + EncAuxRepo(b, false)
      128 +      else                                                    
      129 +        var orn := OrName(PNot(a), PNot(b));                  
      130 +        {Package(orn, 0), Package(orn, 1)} + EncAuxRepo(a, tru
          +e) + EncAuxRepo(b, true)                                      
      131 +    case POr(a, b) =>                                         
      132 +      if !neg then                                            
      133 +        var orn := OrName(a, b);                              
      134 +        {Package(orn, 0), Package(orn, 1)} + EncAuxRepo(a, fal
          +se) + EncAuxRepo(b, false)                                    
      135 +      else EncAuxRepo(a, true) + EncAuxRepo(b, true)          
      136 +    case PNot(g) => EncAuxRepo(g, !neg)                       
      137 +  }                                                           
      138 +                                                              
      139 +  // Definition 4.5.4(a).                                     
      140 +  function PfReduceRepo(repo: set<Package>, pfdeps: PfDepRel):
          + set<Package> {                                               
      141 +    repo + set e, p | e in pfdeps && p in EncAuxRepo(e.1, fals
          +e) :: p                                                       
      142 +  }                                                           
      143 +                                                              
      144 +  // Definition 4.5.4(b): each depender requires its formula's
          + targets,                                                     
      145 +  // plus the global auxiliary edges.                         
      146 +  function PfReduceDeps(pfdeps: PfDepRel): DepRel {           
      147 +    (set e, t | e in pfdeps && t in EncTargets(e.1, false) :: 
          +(e.0, t))                                                     
      148 +    + (set e, ed | e in pfdeps && ed in EncAuxEdges(e.1, false
          +) :: ed)                                                      
      149 +  }                                                           
      150  }

       39  ## Paper claim → Dafny lemma
       40  
       36 -| Paper | Claim | Lemma (all verified) |                      
       41 +| Paper | Claim | Lemma (all verified, no assumes/axioms) |   
       42  |---|---|---|
       38 -| Def 3.2.2 | resolution ordering is a partial order on S(D, r
          -) | `ResLeqRefl`, `ResLeqTrans`, `ResLeqAntisym` (VersionsLemm
          -as.dfy) |                                                     
       39 -| Thm 3.2.7 | version formula reduction is correct | `VfReduct
          -ionCorrect` (VersionsLemmas.dfy) |                            
       40 -| Thm 3.1.4 | NP-hardness via 3-SAT (Appendix B) | `SatGivesRe
          -solution`, `ResolutionGivesSat`, `HardnessCorrect` (HardnessLe
          -mmas.dfy) |                                                   
       41 -| Thm 3.1.4 | NP membership: poly-time checkable | `ValidResol
          -ution` is an executable predicate; `AllResolutions` (Solver.df
          -y) carries an exactness postcondition |                       
       42 -| Thm 4.1.4 | conflict reduction soundness | `ConflictReductio
          -nSound` (ConflictsLemmas.dfy) |                               
       43 -| Thm 4.1.5 | conflict reduction completeness | `ConflictReduc
          -tionComplete` (ConflictsLemmas.dfy) |                         
       44 -| §4.5 | package formulae subsume the core | `CoreEmbedding` (
          -PackageFormulaeLemmas.dfy) |                                  
       45 -| §4.8 | optional deps do not affect resolution, only the buil
          -d graph | `OptionalIrrelevantToResolution`, `BuildGraphMonoton
          -e`, `OptionalEdgeAlwaysPresent` (OptionalLemmas.dfy) |        
       46 -| §4.9 | singular deps embed into the core (restriction) | `Si
          -ngularEmbedding` (SingularLemmas.dfy) |

          -gLemmas.dfy) |

          -ncodingLemmas.dfy) |

          +as) |

          +ionCorrect` (VersionsLemmas) |

       50 -Notes on antisymmetry (Def 3.2.2): the paper's ordering is a p
          -artial order                                                  
       51 -*on resolutions* — antisymmetry uses version uniqueness (Def 3
          -.1.3(c)). On                                                  
       52 -arbitrary package sets the relation is only a preorder; `ResLe
          -qAntisym`                                                     
       53 -makes the needed hypothesis explicit.                         
       58 +The Tseitin-style package formula reduction (Definition 4.5.4)
          + is                                                           
       59 +implemented (`EncTargets`/`EncAuxEdges`/`EncAuxRepo`) and vali
          +dated                                                         
       60 +*exhaustively on the paper's Figure D.1 instance* — the resolv
          +er enumerates                                                 
       61 +the reduced instance's resolutions and they project onto exact
          +ly the                                                        
       62 +formula calculus's resolutions — but the general Theorems 4.5.
          +5/4.5.6 are                                                   
       63 +not mechanised. Likewise §4.6's calculus is implemented and te
          +sted while                                                    
       64 +its reduction (Definition 4.6.3) and the §5.2 composition theo
          +rems are not.                                                 
       65  
       66  ## Modelling choices
       67  
       57 -- **Versions** are naturals (`type Version = nat`), which supp
          -lies the                                                      
       58 -  total order of Definition 3.2.1. The calculus only ever comp
          -ares                                                          
       59 -  versions, so this loses no generality for the mechanised res
          -ults.                                                         
       60 -- **Synthetic names** introduced by reductions (the conflict p
          -ackage                                                        
       61 -  κ_{p,(m,S)} of Def 4.1.3, the root/variable/clause packages 
          -of                                                            
       62 -  Appendix B) are constructors of the `Name` datatype. Constru
          -ctor                                                          
       63 -  injectivity and disjointness give exactly the freshness prop
          -erties the                                                    
       64 -  paper's reductions assume.                                  
       65 -- `ValidResolution` includes `r ⊆ repo` (the paper's "a resolu
          -tion R ⊆ 𝒫"                                                   
       66 -  drawn from the packages that exist).                        
       67 -- The version-formula semantics follows Definition 3.2.3(e) *l
          -iterally*,                                                    
       68 -  including ⟦= v⟧ = {v} (not intersected with the existing ver
          -sions);                                                       
       69 -  `TestVersionFormulae` exercises that corner.                
       68 +- **Versions** are naturals (`type Version = nat`), supplying 
          +the total                                                     
       69 +  order of Definition 3.2.1. Where the paper's reductions need
          + structured                                                   
       70 +  versions — the virtual package reduction encodes the chosen 
          +*provider*                                                    
       71 +  as the intermediate's version (Figure D.2) — the reduction t
          +akes an                                                       
       72 +  injective `enc : Package → Version` as a parameter.         
       73 +- **Synthetic names** introduced by reductions (conflict κ-pac
          +kages,                                                        
       74 +  granular names ⟨n, γ⟩, intermediates ⟨n, v, m⟩, feature pack
          +ages ⟨n, f⟩,                                                  
       75 +  provider intermediates ⟨p, m⟩, Tseitin disjunction/negation 
          +packages)                                                     
       76 +  are constructors of the `Name` datatype; constructor injecti
          +vity and                                                      
       77 +  disjointness give the freshness properties the paper's reduc
          +tions                                                         
       78 +  assume implicitly.                                          
       79 +- **Intermediate naming** in §4.2/§4.3/§4.7 keys intermediates
          + by                                                           
       80 +  (depender, dependee name), exactly as the paper's ⟨n, v, m⟩ 
          +— which                                                       
       81 +  presumes at most one dependency per (depender, name) pair. W
          +e surface                                                     
       82 +  that as the explicit `UniqueDepPerName` precondition (withou
          +t it the                                                      
       83 +  paper's parent-relation theorems are not provable as stated)
          +. Similarly,                                                  
       84 +  `NonemptyDeps` excludes empty version sets, which the reduct
          +ions would                                                    
       85 +  silently drop.                                              
       86 +- **Parent/provider relations:** the §4.3 peer formalisation r
          +euses the                                                     
       87 +  concurrent parent relation ρ ⊆ P × P (child, parent). The §4
          +.7 provider                                                   
       88 +  relation is keyed by the dependency — π ⊆ (P × N) × P — so "
          +exactly one                                                   
       89 +  provider" is expressible per dependency; with the paper's π 
          +⊆ P × P, a                                                    
       90 +  provider selected for one dependency can alias another's.

  Things the mechanisation surfaced about the paper

  - The paper's intermediate names ⟨n, v, m⟩ (§4.2/4.3) silently assume at most 
  one dependency per (depender, dependee-name) pair — without it the
  parent-relation theorems are false as stated (two deps of one package on the
  same name confuse ρ). This is now the explicit UniqueDepPerName precondition.
  - The §4.7 provider relation π ⊆ P × P can't express "exactly one provider per
  dependency" when one selected provider serves two of a package's
  dependencies; I keyed it by dependency, π ⊆ (P × N) × P, and noted this in the
  README.
  - Empty version sets would be silently dropped by the reductions, so
  NonemptyDeps is required.

  Your verification advice worked well: the peer soundness proof was the one
  that fought back, and the fix was exactly your prescription —
  @IsolateAssertions, splitting into per-dependency helper lemmas
  (PeerOneDepExists/PeerOneDepUnique), plus Dafny 4.10's hide * statement to
  stop set-comprehension quantifier blowup. The two-minute limit is now set
  project-wide in dfyconfig.toml.

  Still unmechanised (documented in the README): the general Theorems
  4.5.5/4.5.6, the §4.6 reduction, and §5.2's composition theorems — the
  composition proofs (Concurrent ∘ Features) would be the natural next challenge
  if you want to keep going.

          +ge(t.name, v) in r

      172 +  // The construction of Theorem 4.5.6: witness sets.         
      173 +  // ---------------------------------------------------------
          +------------                                                  
      174 +                                                              
      175 +  // The witness set W(ψ) of Theorem 4.5.6, with De Morgan's l
          +aws realised                                                  
      176 +  // as a polarity flag: the synthetic packages that accompany
          + a resolution                                                 
      177 +  // satisfying ψ (or, at negative polarity, falsifying it). D
          +isjunction                                                    
      178 +  // packages take version 0 when the left disjunct is satisfi
          +ed; negated                                                   
      179 +  // atoms contribute their conflict package at version 1.    
      180 +  function PfWitness(r: set<Package>, f: PFormula, neg: bool):
          + set<Package>                                                 
      181 +    decreases FSize(f)                                        
      182 +  {                                                           
      183 +    match f                                                   
      184 +    case PAtom(n, vs) =>                                      
      185 +      if !neg then {} else {Package(NegName(n, vs), 1)}       
      186 +    case PAnd(a, b) =>                                        
      187 +      if !neg then PfWitness(r, a, false) + PfWitness(r, b, fa
          +lse)                                                          
      188 +      else                                                    
      189 +        var orn := OrName(PNot(a), PNot(b));                  
      190 +        if !PfSat(r, a) then {Package(orn, 0)} + PfWitness(r, 
          +a, true)                                                      
      191 +        else {Package(orn, 1)} + PfWitness(r, b, true)        
      192 +    case POr(a, b) =>                                         
      193 +      if !neg then                                            
      194 +        var orn := OrName(a, b);                              
      195 +        if PfSat(r, a) then {Package(orn, 0)} + PfWitness(r, a
          +, false)                                                      
      196 +        else {Package(orn, 1)} + PfWitness(r, b, false)       
      197 +      else PfWitness(r, a, true) + PfWitness(r, b, true)      
      198 +    case PNot(g) => PfWitness(r, g, !neg)                     
      199 +  }                                                           
      200 +                                                              
      201 +  // Conflict packages forced to version 0 by selected package
          +s: whenever a                                                 
      202 +  // negated atom's conflicting package is in the resolution, 
          +the global                                                    
      203 +  // push edges of Definition 4.5.4(b)(vi) demand its kappa at
          + 0.                                                           
      204 +  function PfPushNegs(r: set<Package>, pfdeps: PfDepRel): set<
          +Package> {                                                    
      205 +    set e, q | e in pfdeps && q in EncAuxRepo(e.1, false) && q
          +.name.NegName?                                                
      206 +      && (exists u :: u in q.name.nscope && Package(q.name.nba
          +se, u) in r)                                                  
      207 +      :: Package(q.name, 0)                                   
      208 +  }                                                           
      209 +                                                              
      210 +  function PfWitnessPart(r: set<Package>, pfdeps: PfDepRel): s
          +et<Package> {                                                 
      211 +    set e, q | e in pfdeps && e.0 in r && q in PfWitness(r, e.
          +1, false) :: q                                                
      212 +  }                                                           
      213 +                                                              
      214 +  // Theorem 4.5.6: R̂ = R ∪ ⋃ W(ψ) (∪ the pushed conflict pack
          +ages).                                                        
      215 +  function PfBuildCore(r: set<Package>, pfdeps: PfDepRel): set
          +<Package> {                                                   
      216 +    r + PfWitnessPart(r, pfdeps) + PfPushNegs(r, pfdeps)      
      217 +  }                                                           
      218  }

      650 +    FeaturesLemmas.BuildFeatDecode(repo, rf, ed.0);           
      651 +    var pe :| pe in rf && pe.0 == Package(ed.0.name.fbase, ed.
          +0.version) && ed.0.name.feat in pe.1;                         
      652 +    assert pe.0 == a.0.0 && a.0.1 in pe.1;                    
      653 +    var v :| v in a.1.versions && ((a.0, a.1), v) in selA && C
          +FSelected(rf, a.1, v);                                        
      654 +    var q :| q in rf && q.0 == Package(a.1.name, v) && a.1.fea
          +ts <= q.1;                                                    
      655 +    assert Package(FeatureName(q.0.name, f), q.0.version) in F
          +eatBuildCore(rf);                                             
      656 +    assert Package(FeatureName(q.0.name, f), q.0.version) == P
          +ackage(FeatureName(a.1.name, f), v);                          
      657 +    assert (Package(FeatureName(a.1.name, f), v), ed.0) in CFR
          +hoAddFeat(adeps, selA);                                       
      658 +    assert Selected(ed, v, rFeat, rho);                       
      659 +                                                              
      660 +    forall v1, v2 | v1 in ed.1.versions && v2 in ed.1.versions
      661 +          && Selected(ed, v1, rFeat, rho) && Selected(ed, v2, 
          +rFeat, rho)                                                   
      662 +      ensures v1 == v2                                        
      663 +    {                                                         
      664 +      AddFeatSelUnique(repo, fsupp, fdeps, adeps, rf, selP, se
          +lA, a, f, v1);                                                
      665 +      AddFeatSelUnique(repo, fsupp, fdeps, adeps, rf, selP, se
          +lA, a, f, v2);                                                
      666 +    }                                                         
      667 +  }                                                           
      668 +                                                              
      669 +  lemma AddFeatSelUnique(repo: set<Package>, fsupp: SupportRel
          +, fdeps: FDepRel, adeps: AddDepRel,                           
      670 +                         rf: FRes, selP: ParamSel, selA: AddSe
          +l,                                                            
      671 +                         a: ((Package, Feature), FDep), f: Fea
          +ture, v: Version)                                             
      672 +    requires PlainFeatureInstance(repo, fsupp, fdeps, adeps)  
      673 +    requires WfFDeps(repo, fsupp, fdeps)                      
      674 +    requires FResInRepo(repo, fsupp, rf)                      
      675 +    requires CFUniqueAdds(adeps)                              
      676 +    requires a in adeps                                       
      677 +    requires (Package(FeatureName(a.1.name, f), v), Package(Fe
          +atureName(a.0.0.name, a.0.1), a.0.0.version))                 
      678 +             in ConcFeatRho(rf, selP, selA, fdeps, adeps)     
      679 +    ensures ((a.0, a.1), v) in selA                           
      680 +  {                                                           
      681 +    var parent := Package(FeatureName(a.0.0.name, a.0.1), a.0.
          +0.version);                                                   
      682 +    RhoFeatFeat(rf, selP, selA, fdeps, adeps, repo, fsupp, Pac
          +kage(FeatureName(a.1.name, f), v), parent);                   
      683 +    var a', f' :| a' in adeps && f' in a'.1.feats             
      684 +          && Package(FeatureName(a'.0.0.name, a'.0.1), a'.0.0.
          +version) == parent                                            
      685 +          && FeatureName(a'.1.name, f') == FeatureName(a.1.nam
          +e, f)                                                         
      686 +          && ((a'.0, a'.1), v) in selA;                       
      687 +    assert a'.0.0 == Package(a'.0.0.name, a'.0.0.version);    
      688 +    assert a.0.0 == Package(a.0.0.name, a.0.0.version);       
      689 +    assert a'.0 == a.0;                                       
      690 +    assert a'.1 == a.1;  // CFUniqueAdds                      
      691 +  }                                                           
      692 +                                                              
      693 +  // ---------------------------------------------------------
          +------------                                                  
      694 +  // The bridge and Theorem 5.2.3.                            
      695 +  // ---------------------------------------------------------
          +------------                                                  
      696 +                                                              
      697 +  lemma BridgeGranularity(repo: set<Package>, fsupp: SupportRe
          +l, g: GranFn, rf: FRes)                                       
      698 +    requires forall p | p in repo :: !p.name.FeatureName?     
      699 +    requires FResInRepo(repo, fsupp, rf)                      
      700 +    requires CFGranularity(g, rf)                             
      701 +    ensures VersionGranularity(g, FeatBuildCore(rf))          
      702 +  {                                                           
      703 +    var rFeat := FeatBuildCore(rf);                           
      704 +    forall p, q | p in rFeat && q in rFeat && p.name == q.name
          + && p.version != q.version                                    
      705 +      ensures g(p.version) != g(q.version)                    
      706 +    {                                                         
      707 +      if p in (set e | e in rf :: e.0) && q in (set e | e in r
          +f :: e.0) {                                                   
      708 +        var e1 :| e1 in rf && p == e1.0;                      
      709 +        var e2 :| e2 in rf && q == e2.0;                      
      710 +      } else if p !in (set e | e in rf :: e.0) && q !in (set e
          + | e in rf :: e.0) {                                          
      711 +        var e1, f1 :| e1 in rf && f1 in e1.1 && p == Package(F
          +eatureName(e1.0.name, f1), e1.0.version);                     
      712 +        var e2, f2 :| e2 in rf && f2 in e2.1 && q == Package(F
          +eatureName(e2.0.name, f2), e2.0.version);                     
      713 +        assert e1.0.name == e2.0.name;                        
      714 +        assert e1.0.version == p.version && e2.0.version == q.
          +version;                                                      
      715 +      } else if p in (set e | e in rf :: e.0) {               
      716 +        var e1 :| e1 in rf && p == e1.0;                      
      717 +        var e2, f2 :| e2 in rf && f2 in e2.1 && q == Package(F
          +eatureName(e2.0.name, f2), e2.0.version);                     
      718 +        assert e1.0 in repo;                                  
      719 +        assert false;  // plain vs FeatureName                
      720 +      } else {                                                
      721 +        var e1, f1 :| e1 in rf && f1 in e1.1 && p == Package(F
          +eatureName(e1.0.name, f1), e1.0.version);                     
      722 +        var e2 :| e2 in rf && q == e2.0;                      
      723 +        assert e2.0 in repo;                                  
      724 +        assert false;                                         
      725 +      }                                                       
      726 +    }                                                         
      727 +  }                                                           
      728 +                                                              
      729 +  @IsolateAssertions                                          
      730 +  lemma Bridge(repo: set<Package>, fsupp: SupportRel, fdeps: F
          +DepRel, adeps: AddDepRel,                                     
      731 +               g: GranFn, root: Package, rf: FRes, selP: Param
          +Sel, selA: AddSel)                                            
      732 +    requires PlainFeatureInstance(repo, fsupp, fdeps, adeps)  
      733 +    requires WfFDeps(repo, fsupp, fdeps)                      
      734 +    requires WfAddDeps(repo, fsupp, adeps)                    
      735 +    requires WfSupp(repo, fsupp)                              
      736 +    requires CFUniqueDeps(fdeps) && CFUniqueAdds(adeps) && CFA
          +ddNotSelf(adeps)                                              
      737 +    requires root in repo                                     
      738 +    requires ValidConcFeatResolution(repo, fsupp, fdeps, adeps
          +, g, root, rf, selP, selA)                                    
      739 +    ensures ValidConcurrentResolution(FeatReduceRepo(repo, fsu
          +pp),                                                          
      740 +                                      FeatReduceDeps(fsupp, fd
          +eps, adeps), g, root,                                         
      741 +                                      FeatBuildCore(rf),      
      742 +                                      ConcFeatRho(rf, selP, se
          +lA, fdeps, adeps))                                            
      743 +  {                                                           
      744 +    var rFeat := FeatBuildCore(rf);                           
      745 +    var rho := ConcFeatRho(rf, selP, selA, fdeps, adeps);     
      746 +    var depsF := FeatReduceDeps(fsupp, fdeps, adeps);         
      747 +                                                              
      748 +    // rFeat ⊆ reduced repository.                            
      749 +    forall p | p in rFeat                                     
      750 +      ensures p in FeatReduceRepo(repo, fsupp)                
      751 +    {                                                         
      752 +      if p in (set e | e in rf :: e.0) {                      
      753 +        var e :| e in rf && p == e.0;                         
      754 +        assert p in repo;                                     
      755 +      } else {                                                
      756 +        var e, f :| e in rf && f in e.1 && p == Package(Featur
          +eName(e.0.name, f), e.0.version);                             
      757 +        assert (e.0, f) in fsupp;                             
      758 +        assert p in FeatPkgs(fsupp);                          
      759 +      }                                                       
      760 +    }                                                         
      761 +                                                              
      762 +    // Root inclusion.                                        
      763 +    var re :| re in rf && re.0 == root;                       
      764 +    assert root in rFeat;                                     
      765 +                                                              
      766 +    // Version granularity.                                   
      767 +    BridgeGranularity(repo, fsupp, g, rf);                    
      768 +                                                              
      769 +    // Parent closure, edge kind by edge kind.                
      770 +    forall ed | ed in depsF && ed.0 in rFeat                  
      771 +      ensures (exists v | v in ed.1.versions :: Selected(ed, v
          +, rFeat, rho))                                                
      772 +           && (forall v1, v2 | v1 in ed.1.versions && v2 in ed
          +.1.versions                                                   
      773 +                 && Selected(ed, v1, rFeat, rho) && Selected(e
          +d, v2, rFeat, rho) :: v1 == v2)                               
      774 +    {                                                         
      775 +      FeatEdgeDecode(fsupp, fdeps, adeps, ed);                
      776 +      if s :| (s in fsupp                                     
      777 +           && ed == (Package(FeatureName(s.0.name, s.1), s.0.v
          +ersion), Dep(s.0.name, {s.0.version}))) {                     
      778 +        BridgeBaseEdge(repo, fsupp, fdeps, adeps, rf, selP, se
          +lA, s);                                                       
      779 +      } else if e :| (e in fdeps && e.1.feats == {} && ed == (
          +e.0, Dep(e.1.name, e.1.versions))) {                          
      780 +        BridgeParamPlainEdge(repo, fsupp, fdeps, adeps, rf, se
          +lP, selA, e);                                                 
      781 +      } else if e, f :| (e in fdeps && f in e.1.feats         
      782 +           && ed == (e.0, Dep(FeatureName(e.1.name, f), e.1.ve
          +rsions))) {                                                   
      783 +        BridgeParamFeatEdge(repo, fsupp, fdeps, adeps, rf, sel
          +P, selA, e, f);                                               
      784 +      } else if a :| (a in adeps && a.1.feats == {}           
      785 +           && ed == (Package(FeatureName(a.0.0.name, a.0.1), a
          +.0.0.version), Dep(a.1.name, a.1.versions))) {                
      786 +        BridgeAddPlainEdge(repo, fsupp, fdeps, adeps, rf, selP
          +, selA, a);                                                   
      787 +      } else {                                                
      788 +        var a, f :| a in adeps && f in a.1.feats              
      789 +              && ed == (Package(FeatureName(a.0.0.name, a.0.1)
          +, a.0.0.version),                                             
      790 +                        Dep(FeatureName(a.1.name, f), a.1.vers
          +ions));                                                       
      791 +        BridgeAddFeatEdge(repo, fsupp, fdeps, adeps, rf, selP,
          + selA, a, f);                                                 
      792 +      }                                                       
      793 +    }                                                         
      794 +  }                                                           
      795 +                                                              
      796 +  // Theorem 5.2.3 (Completeness of the composition).         
      797 +  lemma ConcFeatComplete(repo: set<Package>, fsupp: SupportRel
          +, fdeps: FDepRel, adeps: AddDepRel,                           
      798 +                         g: GranFn, root: Package, rf: FRes, s
          +elP: ParamSel, selA: AddSel)                                  
      799 +    requires PlainFeatureInstance(repo, fsupp, fdeps, adeps)  
      800 +    requires WfFDeps(repo, fsupp, fdeps)                      
      801 +    requires WfAddDeps(repo, fsupp, adeps)                    
      802 +    requires WfSupp(repo, fsupp)                              
      803 +    requires WfAddOwners(fsupp, adeps)                        
      804 +    requires CFUniqueDeps(fdeps) && CFUniqueAdds(adeps) && CFA
          +ddNotSelf(adeps)                                              
      805 +    requires CFNonempty(fdeps, adeps)                         
      806 +    requires root in repo                                     
      807 +    requires ValidConcFeatResolution(repo, fsupp, fdeps, adeps
          +, g, root, rf, selP, selA)                                    
      808 +    ensures ValidResolution(ConcFeatReduceRepo(repo, fsupp, fd
          +eps, adeps, g),                                               
      809 +                            ConcFeatReduceDeps(fsupp, fdeps, a
          +deps, g),                                                     
      810 +                            GPkg(root, g),                    
      811 +                            ConcBuildCore(FeatBuildCore(rf),  
      812 +                                          ConcFeatRho(rf, selP
          +, selA, fdeps, adeps),                                        
      813 +                                          FeatReduceDeps(fsupp
          +, fdeps, adeps), g))                                          
      814 +  {                                                           
      815 +    FeatDepsWf(repo, fsupp, fdeps, adeps);                    
      816 +    FeatDepsUnique(repo, fsupp, fdeps, adeps);                
      817 +    FeatDepsNonempty(fsupp, fdeps, adeps);                    
      818 +    Bridge(repo, fsupp, fdeps, adeps, g, root, rf, selP, selA)
          +;                                                             
      819 +    ConcurrentLemmas.ConcReductionComplete(FeatReduceRepo(repo
          +, fsupp),                                                     
      820 +                                           FeatReduceDeps(fsup
          +p, fdeps, adeps), g, root,                                    
      821 +                                           FeatBuildCore(rf), 
      822 +                                           ConcFeatRho(rf, sel
          +P, selA, fdeps, adeps));                                      
      823 +  }                                                           
      824  }

          +ere) |

       43 -| Def 3.2.2 | resolution ordering is a partial order on S(D, r
          -) | `ResLeqRefl`, `ResLeqTrans`, `ResLeqAntisym` (VersionsLemm
          -as) |                                                         
       44 -| Thm 3.2.7 | version formula reduction is correct | `VfReduct
          -ionCorrect` (VersionsLemmas) |

          -solution`, `ResolutionGivesSat`, `HardnessCorrect` (HardnessLe
          -mmas) |

          -ution` is executable; `AllResolutions` (Solver.dfy) has a prov
          -en exactness contract |

          -flictReductionSound`, `ConflictReductionComplete` (ConflictsLe
          -mmas) |

          -lete | `ConcReductionSound`, `ConcReductionComplete` (Concurre
          -ntLemmas) |

          -`CoreEmulationForward`, `CoreEmulationBackward` (ConcurrentLem
          -mas) |

          - | `PeerReductionSound`, `PeerReductionComplete` (PeersLemmas)
          - |

          -ReductionSound`, `FeatReductionComplete` (FeaturesLemmas) |   
       44 +| Def 3.2.2 | resolution ordering is a partial order on S(D, r
          +) | `ResLeqRefl/Trans/Antisym` (VersionsLemmas) |             
       45 +| Thm 3.2.7 | version formula reduction correct | `VfReduction
          +Correct` (VersionsLemmas) |                                   
       46 +| Thm 3.1.4 | NP-hardness via 3-SAT (App. B) | `SatGivesResolu
          +tion`, `ResolutionGivesSat`, `HardnessCorrect` (HardnessLemmas
          +) |                                                           
       47 +| Thm 3.1.4 | NP membership | executable `ValidResolution`; `A
          +llResolutions` exactness contract (Solver) |                  
       48 +| Thm 4.1.4/4.1.5 | conflict reduction sound & complete | `Con
          +flictReduction{Sound,Complete}` (ConflictsLemmas) |           
       49 +| Thm 4.2.4/4.2.5 | concurrent versions reduction sound & comp
          +lete | `ConcReduction{Sound,Complete}` (ConcurrentLemmas) |   
       50 +| Def 4.2.1 | constant g emulates the core | `CoreEmulation{Fo

● Done — every remaining reduction is now mechanised. Final state: all proofs 
  verified, no assumes/axioms, 21 tests passing (dafny test dfyconfig.toml).

  What this round added

  Theorems 4.5.5/4.5.6 — the Tseitin package-formula reduction, fully proved
  (lemmas/TseitinLemmas.dfy). The soundness invariant shows satisfied encoded
  targets make a formula true (positively) or false (negatively) in the
  restriction; completeness constructs the paper's witness sets W(ψ) — with a
  polarity flag realising De Morgan's laws — plus the conflict packages "pushed"
  to version 0 by selected packages, a detail the paper's construction needs
  but doesn't spell out.

  The §4.6 reduction — Theorems 4.6.4/4.6.5, fully proved
  (lemmas/VariableFormulaeLemmas.dfy). It factors elegantly: variable
  comparisons compile to atoms over synthetic variable packages (one package per
  variable, versions = its values), and a SatTransfer lemma — (r, α) ⊨ f ⟺ r ∪
  α-packages ⊨ compile(f) — composes with the freshly proven Tseitin theorems.
  The assignment is read back off the selected variable packages.

  §5.2 — and a genuine finding. The Concurrent Feature Package Calculus (Def
  5.2.1) is mechanised, and:

  - Theorem 5.2.3 (completeness) is proved (ConcFeatComplete): a bridge lemma
  shows a Concurrent Feature resolution induces a concurrent resolution of the
  feature-reduced instance, then the already-proven Theorem 4.2.5 finishes the
  composition.
  - Theorem 5.2.2 (soundness) is false as stated. The feature reduction achieves
  feature unification via version uniqueness — and granularity relaxes exactly
  that. With one dependency requiring {f1, f2} of d across two majors, a valid
  core resolution of the doubly-reduced instance can select ⟨d,f1⟩@1.0.0 and
  ⟨d,f2⟩@2.0.0 — "feature drift" — and its 4.2.4∘4.4.5 extraction violates
  Definition 5.2.1's closure: no selected version carries both features.
  TestFeatureDrift exhibits this executably: the drift resolution checks as
  core-valid, its concurrent extraction checks as valid, and CFSelected fails
  for every version. The paper's §5.2.1 argument ("the feature reduction is
  version-preserving") establishes that granularity passes through, but misses
  that unification depended on uniqueness.

  The README now documents the full claim→lemma table (every numbered theorem in
  §3–§5 and the appendices is either proved or — in 5.2.2's sole case — refuted
  with an executable witness), the finding, and the implicit paper assumptions
  the mechanisation surfaced as explicit preconditions.

  A natural follow-up if you're interested: a repaired Theorem 5.2.2 — e.g.
  proving soundness under a "feature-coherent resolution" hypothesis, or for
  instances where each dependency requires at most one feature — which would pin
  down exactly how much the paper's claim can be salvaged.

       875 +      assert v1 == v2;  // feature coherence                 
       876 +    } else if s1 in plainPart {                              
       877 +      var e1, v1 :| e1 in fdeps && e1.1.feats == {} && v1 in 
           +e1.1.versions                                                
       878 +            && Selected((e1.0, Dep(e1.1.name, e1.1.versions))
           +, v1, rg, rho)                                               
       879 +            && s1 == ((e1.0, e1.1), v1);                     
       880 +      var e2, f2, v2 :| e2 in fdeps && f2 in e2.1.feats && v2
           + in e2.1.versions                                            
       881 +            && Selected((e2.0, Dep(FeatureName(e2.1.name, f2)
           +, e2.1.versions)), v2, rg, rho)                              
       882 +            && s2 == ((e2.0, e2.1), v2);                     
       883 +      assert e1.1 == e2.1 && e1.1.feats == {} && f2 in e2.1.f
           +eats;                                                        
       884 +      assert false;                                          
       885 +    } else {                                                 
       886 +      var e1, f1, v1 :| e1 in fdeps && f1 in e1.1.feats && v1
           + in e1.1.versions                                            
       887 +            && Selected((e1.0, Dep(FeatureName(e1.1.name, f1)
           +, e1.1.versions)), v1, rg, rho)                              
       888 +            && s1 == ((e1.0, e1.1), v1);                     
       889 +      var e2, v2 :| e2 in fdeps && e2.1.feats == {} && v2 in 
           +e2.1.versions                                                
       890 +            && Selected((e2.0, Dep(e2.1.name, e2.1.versions))
           +, v2, rg, rho)                                               
       891 +            && s2 == ((e2.0, e2.1), v2);                     
       892 +      assert e1.1 == e2.1 && e2.1.feats == {} && f1 in e1.1.f
           +eats;                                                        
       893 +      assert false;                                          
       894 +    }                                                        
       895 +  }                                                          
       896 +                                                             
       897 +  // Likewise for the additional selection.                  
       898 +  lemma SelAFunctional(fsupp: SupportRel, fdeps: FDepRel, ade
           +ps: AddDepRel,                                               
       899 +                       rg: set<Package>, rho: ParentRel)     
       900 +    requires ParentClosure(FeatReduceDeps(fsupp, fdeps, adeps
           +), rg, rho)                                                  
       901 +    requires forall pr | pr in rho :: pr.1 in rg             
       902 +    requires FeatureCoherent(fdeps, adeps, rg, rho)          
       903 +    ensures FunctionalA(CFExtractSelA(adeps, rg, rho))       
       904 +  {                                                          
       905 +    var selA := CFExtractSelA(adeps, rg, rho);               
       906 +    forall s1, s2 | s1 in selA && s2 in selA && s1.0 == s2.0 
       907 +      ensures s1.1 == s2.1                                   
       908 +    {                                                        
       909 +      SelAEntryUnique(fsupp, fdeps, adeps, rg, rho, s1, s2); 
       910 +    }                                                        
       911 +  }                                                          
       912 +                                                             
       913 +  lemma SelAEntryUnique(fsupp: SupportRel, fdeps: FDepRel, ad
           +eps: AddDepRel,                                              
       914 +                        rg: set<Package>, rho: ParentRel,    
       915 +                        s1: (((Package, Feature), FDep), Vers
           +ion), s2: (((Package, Feature), FDep), Version))             
       916 +    requires ParentClosure(FeatReduceDeps(fsupp, fdeps, adeps
           +), rg, rho)                                                  
       917 +    requires forall pr | pr in rho :: pr.1 in rg             
       918 +    requires FeatureCoherent(fdeps, adeps, rg, rho)          
       919 +    requires s1 in CFExtractSelA(adeps, rg, rho)             
       920 +    requires s2 in CFExtractSelA(adeps, rg, rho)             
       921 +    requires s1.0 == s2.0                                    
       922 +    ensures s1.1 == s2.1                                     
       923 +  {                                                          
       924 +    var plainPart := set a, v | a in adeps && a.1.feats == {}
           + && v in a.1.versions                                        
       925 +       && Selected((Package(FeatureName(a.0.0.name, a.0.1), a
           +.0.0.version),                                               
       926 +                    Dep(a.1.name, a.1.versions)), v, rg, rho)
       927 +       :: ((a.0, a.1), v);                                   
       928 +    if s1 in plainPart && s2 in plainPart {                  
       929 +      var a1, v1 :| a1 in adeps && a1.1.feats == {} && v1 in 
           +a1.1.versions                                                
       930 +            && Selected((Package(FeatureName(a1.0.0.name, a1.
           +0.1), a1.0.0.version),                                       
       931 +                         Dep(a1.1.name, a1.1.versions)), v1, 
           +rg, rho)                                                     
       932 +            && s1 == ((a1.0, a1.1), v1);                     
       933 +      var a2, v2 :| a2 in adeps && a2.1.feats == {} && v2 in 
           +a2.1.versions                                                
       934 +            && Selected((Package(FeatureName(a2.0.0.name, a2.
           +0.1), a2.0.0.version),                                       
       935 +                         Dep(a2.1.name, a2.1.versions)), v2, 
           +rg, rho)                                                     
       936 +            && s2 == ((a2.0, a2.1), v2);                     
       937 +      assert a1 == a2;                                       
       938 +      var ed := (Package(FeatureName(a1.0.0.name, a1.0.1), a1
           +.0.0.version),                                               
       939 +                 Dep(a1.1.name, a1.1.versions));             
       940 +      assert ed in FeatReduceDeps(fsupp, fdeps, adeps);      
       941 +      assert ed.0 in rg;                                     
       942 +      assert v1 == v2;                                       
       943 +    } else if s1 !in plainPart && s2 !in plainPart {         
       944 +      var a1, f1, v1 :| a1 in adeps && f1 in a1.1.feats && v1
           + in a1.1.versions                                            
       945 +            && Selected((Package(FeatureName(a1.0.0.name, a1.
           +0.1), a1.0.0.version),                                       
       946 +                         Dep(FeatureName(a1.1.name, f1), a1.1
           +.versions)), v1, rg, rho)                                    
       947 +            && s1 == ((a1.0, a1.1), v1);                     
       948 +      var a2, f2, v2 :| a2 in adeps && f2 in a2.1.feats && v2
           + in a2.1.versions                                            
       949 +            && Selected((Package(FeatureName(a2.0.0.name, a2.
           +0.1), a2.0.0.version),                                       
       950 +                         Dep(FeatureName(a2.1.name, f2), a2.1
           +.versions)), v2, rg, rho)                                    
       951 +            && s2 == ((a2.0, a2.1), v2);                     
       952 +      assert a1 == a2;                                       
       953 +      assert v1 == v2;  // feature coherence                 
       954 +    } else if s1 in plainPart {                              
       955 +      var a1, v1 :| a1 in adeps && a1.1.feats == {} && v1 in 
           +a1.1.versions                                                
       956 +            && Selected((Package(FeatureName(a1.0.0.name, a1.
           +0.1), a1.0.0.version),                                       
       957 +                         Dep(a1.1.name, a1.1.versions)), v1, 
           +rg, rho)                                                     
       958 +            && s1 == ((a1.0, a1.1), v1);                     
       959 +      var a2, f2, v2 :| a2 in adeps && f2 in a2.1.feats && v2
           + in a2.1.versions                                            
       960 +            && Selected((Package(FeatureName(a2.0.0.name, a2.
           +0.1), a2.0.0.version),                                       
       961 +                         Dep(FeatureName(a2.1.name, f2), a2.1
           +.versions)), v2, rg, rho)                                    
       962 +            && s2 == ((a2.0, a2.1), v2);                     
       963 +      assert a1.1 == a2.1;                                   
       964 +      assert false;                                          
       965 +    } else {                                                 
       966 +      var a1, f1, v1 :| a1 in adeps && f1 in a1.1.feats && v1
           + in a1.1.versions                                            
       967 +            && Selected((Package(FeatureName(a1.0.0.name, a1.
           +0.1), a1.0.0.version),                                       
       968 +                         Dep(FeatureName(a1.1.name, f1), a1.1
           +.versions)), v1, rg, rho)                                    
       969 +            && s1 == ((a1.0, a1.1), v1);                     
       970 +      var a2, v2 :| a2 in adeps && a2.1.feats == {} && v2 in 
           +a2.1.versions                                                
       971 +            && Selected((Package(FeatureName(a2.0.0.name, a2.
           +0.1), a2.0.0.version),                                       
       972 +                         Dep(a2.1.name, a2.1.versions)), v2, 
           +rg, rho)                                                     
       973 +            && s2 == ((a2.0, a2.1), v2);                     
       974 +      assert a1.1 == a2.1;                                   
       975 +      assert false;                                          
       976 +    }                                                        
       977 +  }                                                          
       978 +                                                             
       979 +  // A satisfied dependency occurrence: the coherent selectio
           +n pins one                                                   
       980 +  // version whose entry carries all required features.      
       981 +  lemma DepOccurrenceSatisfied(repo: set<Package>, fsupp: Sup
           +portRel,                                                     
       982 +                               fdeps: FDepRel, adeps: AddDepR
           +el,                                                          
       983 +                               rg: set<Package>, rho: ParentR
           +el,                                                          
       984 +                               src: Package, d: FDep)        
       985 +    requires forall p | p in repo :: !p.name.FeatureName?    
       986 +    requires rg <= FeatReduceRepo(repo, fsupp)               
       987 +    requires ParentClosure(FeatReduceDeps(fsupp, fdeps, adeps
           +), rg, rho)                                                  
       988 +    requires src in rg                                       
       989 +    requires d.feats == {} ==>                               
       990 +      (src, Dep(d.name, d.versions)) in FeatReduceDeps(fsupp,
           + fdeps, adeps)                                               
       991 +    requires forall f | f in d.feats ::                      
       992 +      (src, Dep(FeatureName(d.name, f), d.versions)) in FeatR
           +educeDeps(fsupp, fdeps, adeps)                               
       993 +    requires forall f1, f2, v1, v2 |                         
       994 +      f1 in d.feats && f2 in d.feats && v1 in d.versions && v
           +2 in d.versions                                              
       995 +      && Selected((src, Dep(FeatureName(d.name, f1), d.versio
           +ns)), v1, rg, rho)                                           
       996 +      && Selected((src, Dep(FeatureName(d.name, f2), d.versio
           +ns)), v2, rg, rho)                                           
       997 +      :: v1 == v2                                            
       998 +    requires !d.name.FeatureName?                            
       999 +    ensures exists v | v in d.versions ::                    
      1000 +      CFSelected(FeatExtract(rg), d, v)                      
      1001 +      && (d.feats == {} ==> Selected((src, Dep(d.name, d.vers
           +ions)), v, rg, rho))                                         
      1002 +      && (forall f | f in d.feats ::                         
      1003 +            Selected((src, Dep(FeatureName(d.name, f), d.vers
           +ions)), v, rg, rho))                                         
      1004 +  {                                                          
      1005 +    var rf := FeatExtract(rg);                               
      1006 +    if d.feats == {} {                                       
      1007 +      var ed := (src, Dep(d.name, d.versions));              
      1008 +      var v :| v in ed.1.versions && Selected(ed, v, rg, rho)
           +;                                                            
      1009 +      var child := Package(d.name, v);                       
      1010 +      assert (child, FeatSelOf(rg, child)) in rf;            
      1011 +      assert CFSelected(rf, d, v);                           
      1012 +    } else {                                                 
      1013 +      var f0 :| f0 in d.feats;                               
      1014 +      var ed0 := (src, Dep(FeatureName(d.name, f0), d.version
           +s));                                                         
      1015 +      var v :| v in ed0.1.versions && Selected(ed0, v, rg, rh
           +o);                                                          
      1016 +      var fp0 := Package(FeatureName(d.name, f0), v);        
      1017 +      assert fp0 in rg;                                      
      1018 +                                                             
      1019 +      // The base edge of fp0 places the base package in rg. 
      1020 +      FeaturesLemmas.FeatPkgDecode(repo, fsupp, fp0);        
      1021 +      var s := (Package(d.name, v), f0);                     
      1022 +      var bEdge := (fp0, Dep(d.name, {v}));                  
      1023 +      assert bEdge == (Package(FeatureName(s.0.name, s.1), s.
           +0.version), Dep(s.0.name, {s.0.version}));                   
      1024 +      assert bEdge in FeatBaseEdges(fsupp);                  
      1025 +      var w :| w in bEdge.1.versions && Selected(bEdge, w, rg
           +, rho);                                                      
      1026 +      assert w == v;                                         
      1027 +      var base := Package(d.name, v);                        
      1028 +      assert base in rg;                                     
      1029 +                                                             
      1030 +      // Every required feature's package sits at the same ve
           +rsion v.                                                     
      1031 +      var q := (base, FeatSelOf(rg, base));                  
      1032 +      assert q in rf;                                        
      1033 +      forall f | f in d.feats                                
      1034 +        ensures f in q.1 && Selected((src, Dep(FeatureName(d.
           +name, f), d.versions)), v, rg, rho)                          
      1035 +      {                                                      
      1036 +        var edf := (src, Dep(FeatureName(d.name, f), d.versio
           +ns));                                                        
      1037 +        var vf :| vf in edf.1.versions && Selected(edf, vf, r
           +g, rho);                                                     
      1038 +        assert vf == v;  // coherence hypothesis             
      1039 +        assert Package(FeatureName(d.name, f), v) in rg;     
      1040 +      }                                                      
      1041 +      assert CFSelected(rf, d, v);                           
      1042 +    }                                                        
      1043 +  }                                                          
      1044 +                                                             
      1045 +  // The repaired Theorem 5.2.2, from the concurrent level: a
           + concurrent                                                  
      1046 +  // resolution of the feature-reduced instance that is featu
           +re-coherent                                                  
      1047 +  // extracts to a valid Concurrent Feature resolution.      
      1048 +  @IsolateAssertions                                         
      1049 +  lemma ConcFeatExtractSound(repo: set<Package>, fsupp: Suppo
           +rtRel,                                                       
      1050 +                             fdeps: FDepRel, adeps: AddDepRel
           +, g: GranFn,                                                 
      1051 +                             root: Package, rg: set<Package>,
           + rho: ParentRel)                                             
      1052 +    requires PlainFeatureInstance(repo, fsupp, fdeps, adeps) 
      1053 +    requires WfFDeps(repo, fsupp, fdeps)                     
      1054 +    requires root in repo                                    
      1055 +    requires forall pr | pr in rho :: pr.1 in rg             
      1056 +    requires ValidConcurrentResolution(FeatReduceRepo(repo, f
           +supp),                                                       
      1057 +                                       FeatReduceDeps(fsupp, 
           +fdeps, adeps), g, root, rg, rho)                             
      1058 +    requires FeatureCoherent(fdeps, adeps, rg, rho)          
      1059 +    ensures ValidConcFeatResolution(repo, fsupp, fdeps, adeps
           +, g, root,                                                   
      1060 +                                    FeatExtract(rg),         
      1061 +                                    CFExtractSelP(fdeps, rg, 
           +rho),                                                        
      1062 +                                    CFExtractSelA(adeps, rg, 
           +rho))                                                        
      1063 +  {                                                          
      1064 +    var rf := FeatExtract(rg);                               
      1065 +    var selP := CFExtractSelP(fdeps, rg, rho);               
      1066 +    var selA := CFExtractSelA(adeps, rg, rho);               
      1067 +    var depsF := FeatReduceDeps(fsupp, fdeps, adeps);        
      1068 +                                                             
      1069 +    // FResInRepo.                                           
      1070 +    forall e | e in rf                                       
      1071 +      ensures e.0 in repo && forall f | f in e.1 :: (e.0, f) 
           +in fsupp                                                     
      1072 +    {                                                        
      1073 +      var p :| p in rg && !p.name.FeatureName? && e == (p, Fe
           +atSelOf(rg, p));                                             
      1074 +      assert p in FeatReduceRepo(repo, fsupp) && p !in FeatPk
           +gs(fsupp);                                                   
      1075 +      forall f | f in e.1                                    
      1076 +        ensures (e.0, f) in fsupp                            
      1077 +      {                                                      
      1078 +        var q :| q in rg && q.name.FeatureName?              
      1079 +              && q.name.fbase == p.name && q.version == p.ver
           +sion && f == q.name.feat;                                    
      1080 +        FeaturesLemmas.FeatPkgDecode(repo, fsupp, q);        
      1081 +        assert Package(q.name.fbase, q.version) == p;        
      1082 +      }                                                      
      1083 +    }                                                        
      1084 +                                                             
      1085 +    // Root entry.                                           
      1086 +    assert (root, FeatSelOf(rg, root)) in rf;                
      1087 +                                                             
      1088 +    // Feature unification: the feature set is a function of 
           +the package.                                                 
      1089 +    forall e1, e2 | e1 in rf && e2 in rf && e1.0 == e2.0     
      1090 +      ensures e1.1 == e2.1                                   
      1091 +    {                                                        
      1092 +      var p1 :| p1 in rg && !p1.name.FeatureName? && e1 == (p
           +1, FeatSelOf(rg, p1));                                       
      1093 +      var p2 :| p2 in rg && !p2.name.FeatureName? && e2 == (p
           +2, FeatSelOf(rg, p2));                                       
      1094 +      assert p1 == p2;                                       
      1095 +    }                                                        
      1096 +                                                             
      1097 +    // Granularity, inherited from the concurrent resolution.
      1098 +    forall e1, e2 | e1 in rf && e2 in rf                     
      1099 +        && e1.0.name == e2.0.name && e1.0.version != e2.0.ver
           +sion                                                         
      1100 +      ensures g(e1.0.version) != g(e2.0.version)             
      1101 +    {                                                        
      1102 +      assert e1.0 in rg && e2.0 in rg;                       
      1103 +    }                                                        
      1104 +                                                             
      1105 +    SelPFunctional(fsupp, fdeps, adeps, rg, rho);            
      1106 +    SelAFunctional(fsupp, fdeps, adeps, rg, rho);            
      1107 +                                                             
      1108 +    // Parameterised closure.                                
      1109 +    forall pe, e | pe in rf && e in fdeps && e.0 == pe.0     
      1110 +      ensures exists v | v in e.1.versions ::                
      1111 +        ((e.0, e.1), v) in selP && CFSelected(rf, e.1, v)    
      1112 +    {                                                        
      1113 +      assert pe.0 in rg;                                     
      1114 +      if e.1.feats == {} {                                   
      1115 +        assert (e.0, Dep(e.1.name, e.1.versions)) in FeatPara
           +mEdges(fdeps);                                               
      1116 +      }                                                      
      1117 +      forall f | f in e.1.feats                              
      1118 +        ensures (e.0, Dep(FeatureName(e.1.name, f), e.1.versi
           +ons)) in depsF                                               
      1119 +      {                                                      
      1120 +        assert (e.0, Dep(FeatureName(e.1.name, f), e.1.versio
           +ns)) in FeatParamEdges(fdeps);                               
      1121 +      }                                                      
      1122 +      DepOccurrenceSatisfied(repo, fsupp, fdeps, adeps, rg, r
           +ho, e.0, e.1);                                               
      1123 +      var v :| v in e.1.versions && CFSelected(rf, e.1, v)   
      1124 +            && (e.1.feats == {} ==> Selected((e.0, Dep(e.1.na
           +me, e.1.versions)), v, rg, rho))                             
      1125 +            && (forall f | f in e.1.feats ::                 
      1126 +                  Selected((e.0, Dep(FeatureName(e.1.name, f)
           +, e.1.versions)), v, rg, rho));                              
      1127 +      if e.1.feats == {} {                                   
      1128 +        assert ((e.0, e.1), v) in selP;                      
      1129 +      } else {                                               
      1130 +        var f0 :| f0 in e.1.feats;                           
      1131 +        assert ((e.0, e.1), v) in selP;                      
      1132 +      }                                                      
      1133 +    }                                                        
      1134 +                                                             
      1135 +    // Additional closure.                                   
      1136 +    forall pe, a | pe in rf && a in adeps && a.0.0 == pe.0 &&
           + a.0.1 in pe.1                                               
      1137 +      ensures exists v | v in a.1.versions ::                
      1138 +        ((a.0, a.1), v) in selA && CFSelected(rf, a.1, v)    
      1139 +    {                                                        
      1140 +      var p :| p in rg && !p.name.FeatureName? && pe == (p, F
           +eatSelOf(rg, p));                                            
      1141 +      var q :| q in rg && q.name.FeatureName?                
      1142 +            && q.name.fbase == p.name && q.version == p.versi
           +on && a.0.1 == q.name.feat;                                  
      1143 +      var src := Package(FeatureName(a.0.0.name, a.0.1), a.0.
           +0.version);                                                  
      1144 +      assert q == src;                                       
      1145 +      if a.1.feats == {} {                                   
      1146 +        assert (src, Dep(a.1.name, a.1.versions)) in FeatAddE
           +dges(adeps);                                                 
      1147 +      }                                                      
      1148 +      forall f | f in a.1.feats                              
      1149 +        ensures (src, Dep(FeatureName(a.1.name, f), a.1.versi
           +ons)) in depsF                                               
      1150 +      {                                                      
      1151 +        assert (src, Dep(FeatureName(a.1.name, f), a.1.versio
           +ns)) in FeatAddEdges(adeps);                                 
      1152 +      }                                                      
      1153 +      DepOccurrenceSatisfied(repo, fsupp, fdeps, adeps, rg, r
           +ho, src, a.1);                                               
      1154 +      var v :| v in a.1.versions && CFSelected(rf, a.1, v)   
      1155 +            && (a.1.feats == {} ==> Selected((src, Dep(a.1.na
           +me, a.1.versions)), v, rg, rho))                             
      1156 +            && (forall f | f in a.1.feats ::                 
      1157 +                  Selected((src, Dep(FeatureName(a.1.name, f)
           +, a.1.versions)), v, rg, rho));                              
      1158 +      if a.1.feats == {} {                                   
      1159 +        assert ((a.0, a.1), v) in selA;                      
      1160 +      } else {                                               
      1161 +        var f0 :| f0 in a.1.feats;                           
      1162 +        assert ((a.0, a.1), v) in selA;                      
      1163 +      }                                                      
      1164 +    }                                                        
      1165 +  }                                                          
      1166 +                                                             
      1167 +  // The repaired Theorem 5.2.2, end to end: from a core reso
           +lution of the                                                
      1168 +  // doubly-reduced instance, via Theorem 4.2.4, under featur
           +e coherence.                                                 
      1169 +  lemma ConcFeatReductionSoundCoherent(repo: set<Package>, fs
           +upp: SupportRel,                                             
      1170 +                                       fdeps: FDepRel, adeps:
           + AddDepRel, g: GranFn,                                       
      1171 +                                       root: Package, r: set<
           +Package>)                                                    
      1172 +    requires PlainFeatureInstance(repo, fsupp, fdeps, adeps) 
      1173 +    requires WfFDeps(repo, fsupp, fdeps)                     
      1174 +    requires WfAddDeps(repo, fsupp, adeps)                   
      1175 +    requires WfSupp(repo, fsupp)                             
      1176 +    requires WfAddOwners(fsupp, adeps)                       
      1177 +    requires CFUniqueDeps(fdeps) && CFUniqueAdds(adeps) && CF
           +AddNotSelf(adeps)                                            
      1178 +    requires CFNonempty(fdeps, adeps)                        
      1179 +    requires root in repo                                    
      1180 +    requires ValidResolution(ConcFeatReduceRepo(repo, fsupp, 
           +fdeps, adeps, g),                                            
      1181 +                             ConcFeatReduceDeps(fsupp, fdeps,
           + adeps, g), GPkg(root, g), r)                                
      1182 +    requires FeatureCoherent(fdeps, adeps, ConcExtractRes(r, 
           +g),                                                          
      1183 +                             ConcExtractRho(r, FeatReduceDeps
           +(fsupp, fdeps, adeps), g))                                   
      1184 +    ensures ValidConcFeatResolution(repo, fsupp, fdeps, adeps
           +, g, root,

● The repaired theorem is fully proved and documented. Final state: all proofs 
  verified, 0 errors, no assumes/axioms, 21 tests passing.

  The repaired Theorem 5.2.2 (all machine-checked)

  FeatureCoherent (src/ConcurrentFeatures.dfy) names the exact property version
  uniqueness was silently providing: for each dependency occurrence, every
  required feature's edge selects the same dependee version under the parent
  relation.

  Three new verified results in lemmas/ConcurrentFeaturesLemmas.dfy:

  - ConcFeatExtractSound — the concurrent-level half: a feature-coherent
  concurrent resolution of the feature-reduced instance extracts to a valid
  Concurrent Feature resolution, with selection witnesses
  CFExtractSelP/CFExtractSelA read off the parent relation. The key step
  (DepOccurrenceSatisfied) re-derives feature unification from coherence + the
  base edges, where the original proof used version uniqueness.
  - ConcFeatReductionSoundCoherent — the end-to-end repaired theorem: core
  resolution of the doubly-reduced instance → Theorem 4.2.4 (already proven) →
  coherence hypothesis → valid S_γF member.
  - CoherentWhenSingleFeature — coherence is automatic when no dependency
  requires more than one feature, so soundness holds unconditionally for that
  syntactic class. Notably, the repaired soundness needs none of the CFUnique*
  side conditions at the concurrent level — the dependency-keyed selections
  carry the disambiguation.

  The tests now close the loop in both directions: TestConcFeatFigure9
  round-trips Figure 9 through Theorem 5.2.3's construction and back through the
  repaired soundness extraction; TestFeatureDrift confirms the drift resolution
  is exactly a coherence failure (expect !FeatureCoherent(...)).

  Documentation

  FINDINGS.md is the standalone write-up: the affected claim, why the paper's
  "version-preserving" argument is insufficient (unification ≠ preservation),
  the concrete counterexample with the drifted resolution spelled out, why real
  Cargo doesn't hit this (its resolver unifies per dependency, not per feature
  edge), the verified repair, an alternative reduction-level repair (shared
  per-dependency intermediates, à la the §4.3 peer reduction — making drift
  unrepresentable at the cost of extension-aware reductions, which §5.2.2 of the
  paper itself contemplates), and an honest caveat that Definition 5.2.1 was
  reconstructed from a lossy PDF extraction — while noting the counterexample
  violates the carried-over Definition 4.4.3(b) directly, which survives any
  reasonable reading.

  The README's claim table now lists 5.2.2 (refuted, with pointer), 5.2.2′
  (repaired, proved), and 5.2.3 (proved).

  With that, every numbered theorem in §3, §4, §5, and Appendices B–C of the
  paper is either machine-checked as stated, or — for Theorem 5.2.2 alone —
  refuted by an executable witness and re-proved under an explicit, named
  hypothesis. If you ever want to take the finding further, the natural next
  step would be mechanising the alternative reduction-level repair and showing
  it makes the unmodified theorem statement true.
